‚Źļ Dust and Daisies Tours ‚ÄĒ Discovery Report

  What it is

  Client website for a Namaqualand tour company (Springbok, Northern Cape).
  Laravel 13 + Filament 5 + Fabricator page builder with a "Desert Journal"
  editorial theme.

  Current state ‚ÄĒ ~70% complete

  Built:
  - Admin panel with site settings
  - 7 page blocks (Hero, TextImage, CTA, CardGrid, FAQ, Gallery, Contact)
  - 6 content pages seeded (Home, Day Tours, Hiking Trails, About, Gallery,
  Contact)
  - Desert Journal theme (custom CSS, Google Fonts, GSAP animations)
  - 62 gallery images migrated from production WordPress site
  - Lightbox gallery with masonry layout

  Single commit ‚ÄĒ all work so far is in one initial commit with uncommitted
  changes on top.

  What's missing (launch blockers)

  1. Contact form ‚ÄĒ block exists but no submission/email logic
  2. SEO ‚ÄĒ no meta tags, Open Graph, or sitemap
  3. Favicon & manifest ‚ÄĒ missing
  4. Error pages ‚ÄĒ no custom 404/500
  5. Tests ‚ÄĒ only example stubs
  6. Mobile QA ‚ÄĒ design not verified on mobile
  7. Deployment ‚ÄĒ no production hosting config

  Suggested Linear tasks

  Design Overhaul Summary

  Aesthetic: "Desert Editorial" ‚ÄĒ luxury travel magazine meets Namaqualand
  landscape

  Key changes:

  (Reey-Regular.woff2, .woff, .otf). Until then, Caveat is the fallback.

  title/description and display them as structured metadata pills with icons
  - No more washi tape, coffee stains, ruled lines, torn paper edges ‚ÄĒ replaced
  with clean editorial layout

  storage)

  orange
  - Buttons ‚ÄĒ btn-primary (filled) and btn-outline variants with hover lift
  effects
  - Gallery ‚ÄĒ cleaner masonry with subtle zoom on hover, refined lightbox
  - Footer ‚ÄĒ 4-column layout with social icon boxes

  1. php artisan migrate:fresh --seed
  2. Download Reey font from fontsquirrel.com/fonts/reey ‚Üí put files in
  public/fonts/
  3. npm run dev to see changes
